[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#development-bounties-future)

Development Bounties (Future)

*   **Plan:** Open bounties for specific improvements and features
    
*   **Goal:** Reward contributions that strengthen the ecosystem
    
*   **Timeline:** Takes time to set up properly
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#community-and-support)

Community & Support


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#official-channels)

Official Channels

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
     - Talk directly with developers and modders
    
*   **Discord (CurseForge):** [CurseForge UGC Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/S3EaZArYz2)
     - User-generated content focus
    
*   **X / Reddit:** Tweet at @Hytale or post on Hytale subreddits
    
*   **Official Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
     - Latest updates and strategy posts
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#what-to-expect)

What to Expect

*   **Early Access Reality:** Tools are uneven, documentation is incomplete, some workflows are frustrating
    
*   **Rapid Improvements:** Developers are fixing issues as they come in
    
*   **Transparency:** Developers commit to being honest about what's ready and what's not
    
*   **Your Feedback Matters:** Hold developers accountable, demand answers, provide feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#important-warnings)

Important Warnings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#data-safety)

Data Safety

> **Critical:** Hytale is in true Early Access. There are crashes, and some can cause **data loss**.

**Practical Advice:**

*   **Take frequent backups** of your savegames and creations
    
*   Treat this phase as valuable but **not yet safe for irreplaceable work**
    
*   Automatic backup solutions are being developed
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#current-limitations)

Current Limitations

*   Missing editing capabilities for some features
    
*   Client behavior not fully exposed to server
    
*   Some tools are rough, inconsistent, or painful to work with
    
*   Modding maturity varies wildly depending on what you're building
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#long-term-vision)

Long-Term Vision


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#node-editors-coming)

Node Editors (Coming)

*   **Purpose:** Visual editors for complex JSON assets
    
*   **Target:** NPCs, Interactions, World Generation
    
*   **Integration:** Directly into Hytale Asset Editor
    
*   **Goal:** Unified creator suite instead of patchwork tools
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#visual-scripting-core-pillar)

Visual Scripting (Core Pillar)

*   **Timeline:** Long-term priority
    
*   **Features:**
    
    *   Sandboxed, safe environment for sharing logic
        
    *   Great learnability for all skill levels
        
    *   Programmers can extend with performance-critical nodes
        
    *   Eventually: Visual scripting directly in the 3D world
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#first-party-server-network)

First-Party Server Network

*   **Plan:** Hypixel-style minigames network
    
*   **Purpose:**
    
    *   Validate modding tools at scale
        
    *   Share code and assets for learning
        
    *   Ensure playable content during early days
        
    
*   **Note:** Not trying to compete with community servers
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#getting-started)

Getting Started


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#for-content-creators-no-coding)

For Content Creators (No Coding)

1.  Start with **Packs** - Create blocks, items, and content using JSON
    
2.  Use the **Asset Editor** to modify properties visually
    
3.  Learn **Blockbench** for custom models and textures
    
4.  Follow the [Getting Started with Packs](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs)
     guide
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#for-developers-java)

For Developers (Java)

1.  Learn **Java programming** fundamentals
    
2.  Set up your development environment (IntelliJ IDEA recommended)
    
3.  Clone the [Plugin Templatearrow-up-right](https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin)
    
4.  Follow the [Getting Started with Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/07-getting-started-with-plugins)
     guide
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#for-advanced-users)

For Advanced Users

1.  Explore **Bootstrap/Early Plugins** for low-level modifications
    
2.  Study the decompiled server source (or wait for official release)
    
3.  Follow the [Bootstrap/Early Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins)
     guide
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#closing-words)

Closing Words


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_From Slikey (Technical Director):_

> "If you're willing to join us in this phase - bugs, rough edges and all - you won't just be modding Hytale. You'll be shaping what Hytale modding becomes."

This documentation aims to help you navigate the current state of Hytale modding while preparing you for the exciting future ahead.

# Plugin Project Template | Hytale Modding Documentation

A minimal, production-ready template for creating Hytale plugins with modern build tools and automated testing.

**GitHub Repository:** [realBritakee/hytale-template-pluginarrow-up-right](https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Hytale Plugin Template is a ready-to-use project structure that builds immediately without any modifications. It includes modern development tools, automated server testing, and CI/CD workflows to help you start developing plugins quickly.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#key-features)

Key Features

✅ **Builds Out-of-the-Box** - Clone and run `./gradlew shadowJar` immediately ✅ **Modern Build System** - Gradle 9.2.0 with Kotlin DSL ✅ **Java 25 Support** - Latest Java features ✅ **Automated Server Testing** - Custom Gradle plugin for one-command testing ✅ **ShadowJar Integration** - Automatic dependency bundling ✅ **CI/CD Ready** - GitHub Actions workflow included ✅ **Minimal Structure** - Only essential files, write your own code

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#quick-start)

Quick Start


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   **Java 25 JDK** - [Download herearrow-up-right](https://www.oracle.com/java/technologies/downloads/)
    
*   **IntelliJ IDEA** - [Download herearrow-up-right](https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/download/)
     (Community Edition works)
    
*   **Git** - [Download herearrow-up-right](https://git-scm.com/)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-1.-clone-the-template)

1\. Clone the Template

Copy

    git clone https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin.git
    cd hytale-template-plugin

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-2.-build-immediately-no-changes-needed)

2\. Build Immediately (No Changes Needed!)

The template works out-of-the-box:

Copy

    # Windows
    gradlew.bat shadowJar
    
    # Linux/Mac
    ./gradlew shadowJar

Your plugin JAR will be in: `build/libs/TemplatePlugin-1.0.0.jar`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-3.-customize-your-plugin)

3\. Customize Your Plugin

When ready to customize, edit these files:

`**settings.gradle.kts**`**:**

Copy

    rootProject.name = "your-plugin-name"

`**gradle.properties**`**:**

Copy

    pluginGroup=com.yourname
    pluginVersion=1.0.0
    pluginDescription=Your plugin description

`**src/main/resources/manifest.json**`**:**

Copy

    {
      "Group": "YourName",
      "Name": "YourPluginName",
      "Main": "com.yourname.yourplugin.YourPlugin"
    }

**Rename the main plugin class:**

*   Rename `src/main/java/com/example/templateplugin/TemplatePlugin.java`
    
*   Update package name to match your `pluginGroup`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-4.-implement-your-plugin)

4\. Implement Your Plugin

Write your plugin code in `src/main/java/`:

*   Commands
    
*   Event listeners
    
*   Services
    
*   Storage
    
*   Utilities
    

See [Advanced Plugin Patterns](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns)
 and [Common Plugin Features](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/14-common-plugin-features)
 for examples.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#project-structure)

Project Structure


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    hytale-template-plugin/
    ├── .github/workflows/
    │   └── build.yml                    # CI/CD workflow
    ├── buildSrc/
    │   ├── build.gradle.kts             # Custom plugin configuration
    │   └── src/main/kotlin/
    │       └── RunHytalePlugin.kt       # Automated server testing
    ├── gradle/wrapper/
    │   ├── gradle-wrapper.jar           # Gradle wrapper binary
    │   └── gradle-wrapper.properties    # Gradle 9.2.0 configuration
    ├── src/main/
    │   ├── java/com/example/templateplugin/
    │   │   └── TemplatePlugin.java      # Minimal main class (example)
    │   └── resources/
    │       ├── manifest.json            # Plugin metadata
    │       └── config.json              # Example configuration
    ├── .gitignore                       # Git ignore rules
    ├── build.gradle.kts                 # Build configuration
    ├── gradle.properties                # Project properties
    ├── gradlew                          # Gradle wrapper (Unix)
    ├── gradlew.bat                      # Gradle wrapper (Windows)
    ├── settings.gradle.kts              # Project settings
    ├── LICENSE                          # MIT License
    └── README.md                        # Documentation

**Note:** This is a minimal template. Create your own folder structure as needed:

*   `commands/` - For command implementations
    
*   `listeners/` - For event listeners
    
*   `services/` - For business logic
    
*   `storage/` - For data persistence
    
*   `utils/` - For utility classes
    
*   `config/` - For configuration management
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#automated-server-testing)

Automated Server Testing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The template includes a custom Gradle plugin for automated server testing. This feature is documented in detail in [Gradle Automation & Testing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/13-gradle-automation-testing)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#quick-usage)

Quick Usage

**Configure in** `**build.gradle.kts**`**:**

Copy

    runHytale {
        jarUrl = "url to hytale server jar"
    }

**Run the server:**

Copy

    # Windows
    gradlew.bat runServer
    
    # Linux/Mac
    ./gradlew runServer

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#what-it-does)

What It Does

1.  ✅ Downloads the Hytale server JAR (cached for future runs)
    
2.  ✅ Compiles your plugin with `shadowJar`
    
3.  ✅ Copies the plugin to `run/plugins/`
    
4.  ✅ Starts the server with interactive console
    
5.  ✅ Supports debug mode: `./gradlew runServer -Pdebug`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#features)

Features

*   **Smart Caching** - Downloads server JAR once, reuses forever
    
*   **Auto-Deploy** - Builds and deploys your plugin automatically
    
*   **Interactive Console** - Type commands directly in the terminal
    
*   **Debug Support** - Connect your IDE debugger to port 5005
    
*   **Clean Workspace** - Server files in `run/` directory (gitignored)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#development-workflow)

Development Workflow


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#building)

Building

Copy

    # Compile only
    ./gradlew compileJava
    
    # Build plugin JAR
    ./gradlew shadowJar
    
    # Clean and rebuild
    ./gradlew clean shadowJar

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#testing)

Testing

Copy

    # Run server with your plugin
    ./gradlew runServer
    
    # Run unit tests
    ./gradlew test
    
    # Clean test server
    rm -rf run/

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#debugging)

Debugging

Copy

    # Run server in debug mode
    ./gradlew runServer -Pdebug
    
    # Then connect your IDE debugger to localhost:5005

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#adding-dependencies)

Adding Dependencies


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Edit `build.gradle.kts`:

Copy

    dependencies {
        // Hytale API (provided by server)
        compileOnly(files("libs/hytale-server.jar"))
        
        // Your dependencies (will be bundled)
        implementation("com.google.code.gson:gson:2.10.1")
        implementation("org.jetbrains:annotations:24.1.0")
        
        // Test dependencies
        testImplementation("org.junit.jupiter:junit-jupiter:5.10.0")
        testRuntimeOnly("org.junit.platform:junit-platform-launcher")
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#dependency-relocation)

Dependency Relocation

To avoid conflicts with other plugins, relocate your dependencies:

Copy

    tasks {
        shadowJar {
            // Relocate dependencies to avoid conflicts
            relocate("com.google.gson", "com.yourplugin.libs.gson")
            relocate("org.apache.commons", "com.yourplugin.libs.commons")
            
            // Minimize JAR size (removes unused classes)
            minimize()
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#ci-cd-with-github-actions)

CI/CD with GitHub Actions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The template includes a GitHub Actions workflow (`.github/workflows/build.yml`) that:

1.  ✅ Builds your plugin on every push
    
2.  ✅ Runs tests
    
3.  ✅ Uploads artifacts
    
4.  ✅ Creates releases when you tag
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#creating-a-release)

Creating a Release

Copy

    git tag v1.0.0
    git push origin v1.0.0

GitHub Actions will automatically build and create a release with your plugin JAR.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#workflow-features)

Workflow Features

*   **Multi-OS Testing** - Builds on Ubuntu, Windows, and macOS
    
*   **Java 25 Support** - Uses the latest Java version
    
*   **Artifact Upload** - Saves built JARs for download
    
*   **Release Automation** - Automatically creates GitHub releases
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#customization-examples)

Customization Examples


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#custom-build-configuration)

Custom Build Configuration

**Change Java version:**

Copy

    java {
        toolchain {
            languageVersion.set(JavaLanguageVersion.of(21))
        }
    }
    
    tasks {
        compileJava {
            options.release = 21
        }
    }

**Add custom repositories:**

Copy

    repositories {
        mavenLocal()
        mavenCentral()
        maven("https://repo.example.com/releases")
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#custom-gradle-tasks)

Custom Gradle Tasks

**Add a custom task:**

Copy

    tasks.register("copyToServer") {
        group = "deployment"
        description = "Copy plugin to local server"
        
        doLast {
            val serverDir = File("C:/HytaleServer/plugins")
            val pluginJar = tasks.shadowJar.get().outputs.files.singleFile
            pluginJar.copyTo(File(serverDir, pluginJar.name), overwrite = true)
            println("Plugin copied to server!")
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#recommended-folder-structure)

Recommended Folder Structure


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you start developing, organize your code like this:

Copy

    src/main/java/com/yourname/yourplugin/
    ├── YourPlugin.java              # Main class
    ├── commands/
    │   ├── CommandManager.java      # Command registration
    │   ├── HelpCommand.java
    │   └── ReloadCommand.java
    ├── listeners/
    │   ├── PlayerJoinListener.java
    │   └── BlockBreakListener.java
    ├── services/
    │   ├── PlayerService.java       # Business logic
    │   └── DataService.java
    ├── storage/
    │   ├── PlayerStorage.java       # Data persistence
    │   └── ConfigStorage.java
    ├── config/
    │   ├── PluginConfig.java        # Configuration classes
    │   └── Messages.java
    └── utils/
        ├── TextUtils.java           # Utility methods
        └── TimeUtils.java

See [Advanced Plugin Patterns](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns)
 for implementation details.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#best-practices)

Best Practices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#do)

✅ DO:

*   Use the Service-Storage pattern for data management
    
*   Write unit tests for your business logic
    
*   Use structured logging (not `System.out.println`)
    
*   Handle errors gracefully with try-catch blocks
    
*   Document your public API with JavaDoc
    
*   Version your releases semantically (1.0.0, 1.1.0, etc.)
    
*   Use dependency injection where possible
    
*   Keep your main class minimal
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#dont)

❌ DON'T:

*   Hardcode configuration values
    
*   Block the main thread with heavy operations
    
*   Ignore exceptions or use empty catch blocks
    
*   Use deprecated APIs
    
*   Commit sensitive data (API keys, passwords)
    
*   Mix business logic with storage logic
    
*   Use static variables for state management
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#build-fails)

Build Fails

Copy

    # Clean and rebuild
    ./gradlew clean build --refresh-dependencies
    
    # Check Gradle version
    ./gradlew --version
    
    # Update Gradle wrapper
    ./gradlew wrapper --gradle-version=9.2.0

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#server-wont-start)

Server Won't Start

1.  Check that `jarUrl` in `build.gradle.kts` is correct
    
2.  Verify Java 25 is installed: `java -version`
    
3.  Check logs in `run/logs/`
    
4.  Ensure the server JAR is compatible
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#plugin-not-loading)

Plugin Not Loading

1.  Verify `manifest.json` has correct `Main` class path
    
2.  Check server logs for errors
    
3.  Ensure all dependencies are bundled in JAR
    
4.  Verify the plugin JAR is in `run/plugins/`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#gradle-daemon-issues)

Gradle Daemon Issues

Copy

    # Stop all Gradle daemons
    ./gradlew --stop
    
    # Rebuild
    ./gradlew clean shadowJar

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#migration-from-other-templates)

Migration from Other Templates


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're migrating from another template:

1.  **Copy your source code** to `src/main/java/`
    
2.  **Update** `**manifest.json**` with your plugin metadata
    
3.  **Copy dependencies** to `build.gradle.kts`
    
4.  **Update package names** to match your group
    
5.  **Test the build** with `./gradlew shadowJar`
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#related-documentation)

     - Practical features

     - Server testing details

# Blockbench Modeling Guide | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [An Introduction to Making Models for Hytalearrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/12/an-introduction-to-making-models-for-hytale)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#introduction)

Introduction


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide covers the official Hytale art style and best practices for creating models using Blockbench. Written by Thomas Frick (Art Director), this represents a decade of art direction for Hytale.

> **Note:** _"These are best practices; you don't have to follow them strictly. You are the masters of your own craft, and there is no good or bad way to create as long as you are having fun."_

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#hytale-art-style)

Hytale Art Style


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#definition)

Definition

**"A modern, stylized voxel game, with retro pixel-art textures"**

Hytale's art style combines:

*   Modern game engine capabilities
    
*   Charm of old-school pixel art
    
*   Intersection of low-definition pixel art and hand-painted 3D
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#the-four-art-pillars)

The Four Art Pillars


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every piece of content in Hytale is evaluated against these core pillars:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-1.-immersive)

1\. Immersive

*   World feels alive, digital nature vanishes
    
*   Motion and detail everywhere
    
*   Wind blows in leaves, creatures wander, clouds travel
    
*   World reacts to the player
    
*   Creatures interact, eyes express emotion
    
*   Lasting impression on players' memories
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-2.-fantasy)

2\. Fantasy

*   Deeply fantasy but not limited to medieval
    
*   Art style remains consistent across universes and themes
    
*   Each character has unique personality and twist
    
*   Popular archetypes are reimagined
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-3.-stylized)

3\. Stylized

*   Iconic and easily identifiable proportions
    
*   Carefully selected color palette
    
*   Players can read the world regardless of clutter
    
*   **Simplicity is key** - doesn't mean low quality
    
*   Takes many iterations to achieve consistency
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-4.-flexible)

4\. Flexible

*   Composed of primitive shapes (cubes and quads)
    
*   Easy to understand how models are made
    
*   Technical structure is simple to comprehend and iterate
    
*   **Empowering user creativity** - true goal of Hytale
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#getting-started)

Getting Started


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#download-required-tools)

Download Required Tools

1.  **Blockbench** - [blockbench.netarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/)
    
2.  **Hytale Blockbench Plugin** - [Hytale Pluginarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale_plugin)
    
3.  **Plugin Source Code** - [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/JannisX11/hytale-blockbench-plugin)
    

> **Important:** The Blockbench plugin is in Early Access. You might encounter bugs, but it will continue to improve.

**Plugin Features:**

*   Maintains consistent pixel ratio across textures
    
*   Exports models and animations in correct format
    
*   Quality-of-life improvements
    
*   Tailored to Hytale engine needs
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#geometry-constraints)

Geometry Constraints


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#primitives)

Primitives

Hytale models use **only 2 primitives:**

1.  **Cubes** (6 sides)
    
2.  **Quads** (2 sides)
    

**Not Allowed:**

*   ❌ Edge loops
    
*   ❌ Special topology
    
*   ❌ Triangles
    
*   ❌ Pyramids
    
*   ❌ Other traditional modeling shapes
    
*   ❌ **No spheres allowed!**
    

**Benefits:**

*   Easy to make, unwrap, and animate
    
*   No weight painting required
    
*   No rigging required
    
*   No 3D art degree required to start
    
*   Blockbench plugin helps maintain simplicity
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#hytale-proportions)

Hytale Proportions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#character-bodies)

Character Bodies

*   **Not realistic** - small, bulky, and cartoony
    
*   Supports chunky style used throughout the game
    
*   Blocks and furniture are "toylike"
    
*   Pure and iconic shapes
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#bone-naming-convention)

Bone Naming Convention

*   Bones must be properly named for animation system
    
*   Once bones are correctly named, they animate in-game automatically
    
*   Refer to official player hierarchy for examples
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#triangle-count-polygon-budget)

Triangle Count (Polygon Budget)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#philosophy)

Philosophy

*   Work as simply as possible
    
*   Increase geometry only when needed to improve silhouette
    
*   Stylistic choice + performance reasons
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#performance-context)

Performance Context

*   Hytale renders **several thousand blocks and voxels simultaneously**
    
*   Results in **several million triangles per frame**
    
*   Triangles are major contributor to FPS loss
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#optimization-requirements)

Optimization Requirements

*   Artists must ensure models are **highly optimized**
    
*   Minimize impact on GPU
    
*   Every triangle counts
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texture-size-and-density)

Texture Size and Density


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texture-requirements)

Texture Requirements

*   **Non-square textures allowed**
    
*   Must be **multiples of 32px** (32, 64, 96, 128, etc.)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texel-density-options)

Texel Density Options

You have **two options** when modeling:

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#option-1-character-attachment)

Option 1: Character/Attachment

*   **Density:** 64px per unit
    
*   **Use For:**
    
    *   Characters
        
    *   Cosmetics
        
    *   Tools
        
    *   Weapons
        
    *   Food items
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#option-2-prop-block)

Option 2: Prop/Block

*   **Density:** 32px per unit
    
*   **Use For:**
    
    *   Cubes
        
    *   Furniture
        
    *   Props
        
    *   Any non-character objects
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#why-higher-density-for-characters)

Why Higher Density for Characters?

**Reasons for 64px density:**

1.  **Emotion Conveyance** - Details on skin, tattoos, makeup, eye/mouth motion
    
2.  **Close-Up Viewing** - Faces seen very close, especially in first-person
    
3.  **Scene Readability** - Characters detach from environment, attract player's eyes
    
4.  **Cosmetic Details** - More options for logos, materials, textures, ornaments
    
5.  **First-Person Immersion** - Hand/weapon/tool looks better close to camera
    

> **Note:** Many avatar customization features will unlock progressively during Early Access.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#stretching-geometry)

Stretching Geometry


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#when-to-use-stretching)

When to Use Stretching

*   Fine adjustments (e.g., avoid Z-fighting when geometry overlaps)
    
*   Slightly resize something
    
*   Work around pixel density limitations
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#stretching-limits)

Stretching Limits

*   **Avoid:** Going under **0.7X** or over **1.3X** stretch on one axis
    
*   Beyond these limits, pixel stretching becomes obvious
    
*   Use sparingly and carefully
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texturing-brushes)

Texturing Brushes


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#recommended-brushes)

Recommended Brushes

You don't need many special brushes! Use any painting software:

*   Photoshop
    
*   GIMP
    
*   Clip Studio
    
*   Affinity
    
*   Krita
    
*   Blockbench
    
*   Procreate
    

**Two Simple Brushes:**

1.  **Pencil Brush**
    
    *   Opacity on for details
        
    *   Use for color-blocking
        
    
2.  **Round Soft Brush**
    
    *   Opacity pressure on
        
    *   For softening surfaces and creating volume
        
    *   Use for smoothing and shading
        
    
3.  **Opacity Pencil**
    
    *   For polish and final details
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texturing-philosophy)

Texturing Philosophy

*   Treat each texture as an **"illustration"**
    
*   Paint/bake shadows, ambient occlusion, and highlights directly into texture
    
*   Simulate more complex lighting than exists in-game
    
*   Create illusion of detail
    
*   **Avoid:**
    
    *   Noise
        
    *   Too much grain
        
    *   Perfectly flat surfaces
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#color-picking-guidelines)

Color Picking Guidelines


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#color-theory-rules)

Color Theory Rules

**Do:**

*   ✅ Add color in shadows (hint of purple makes models vibrant)
    
*   ✅ Use nuanced, saturated shadows
    
*   ✅ Test colors in-game once available
    

**Don't:**

*   ❌ Use pure white (#FFFFFF)
    
*   ❌ Use pure black (#000000)
    
*   ❌ Create purely desaturated shadows
    

**Why Avoid Pure White/Black:**

*   Breaks lighting in-game
    
*   Adds too much contrast
    
*   Ruins value balance
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#shading-mode-and-materials)

Shading Mode and Materials


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#character-models)

Character Models

*   **Recommendation:** Disable side shadows in Blockbench
    
*   Avoids hard edge effect on body
    
*   Better for simulating curvy organic volumes
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#in-game-materials)

In-Game Materials

*   Tight set of material types (shading modes)
    
*   Performance and style reasons
    
*   Blockbench can't display shading modes yet
    
*   Can set and export shading modes for each node
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#hytale-renderer)

Hytale Renderer


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#rendering-approach)

Rendering Approach

*   **Not using PBR workflows** (no roughness, normal maps, displacement)
    
*   Tailored to elevate unique art style
    
*   Avoids effects that damage handcrafted texture style
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#rendering-features)

Rendering Features

*   Paint lights and shadows inside textures
    
*   Real lights/shadows bring everything together
    
*   In-house light propagation techniques
    
*   Selective shaders and post-processing:
    
    *   Bloom
        
    *   Depth of Field
        
    *   Ambient Occlusion (SSAO)
        
    *   Shadowmap
        
    *   Fog
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#quality-standard)

Quality Standard

*   Models should look good **without any effects**
    
*   Effects are "cherry on top"
    
*   Makes Hytale feel cozy and vibrant
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#future-rendering-features)

Future Rendering Features

*   Light propagation improvements
    
*   Colorimetry and gamma features
    
*   Color grading control
    
*   Godrays
    
*   Transparent glass
    
*   Many other surprises
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#official-tutorial-videos)

Official Tutorial Videos


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Magma Golem Tutorial** by Thomas Frick (Art Director)

*   Concepting process
    
*   Modeling workflow
    
*   Available on official Hytale channels
    

**Download Official Models:**

*   [Hytale Model Examples.ziparrow-up-right](https://cdn.hytale.com/Hytale%20Model%20Examples.zip)
    
*   Includes selection of official models for study and tinkering
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#best-practices-summary)

Best Practices Summary


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#geometry)

Geometry

1.  Use only cubes and quads
    
2.  Keep triangle count low
    
3.  Optimize for performance
    
4.  No spheres!
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#textures)

Textures

1.  Multiples of 32px only
    
2.  Choose correct density (64px for characters, 32px for props)
    
3.  Avoid pure white and pure black
    
4.  Paint shadows and highlights into texture
    
5.  Add color to shadows
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#workflow)

Workflow

1.  Start simple
    
2.  Iterate to improve silhouette
    
3.  Test in-game when possible
    
4.  Follow art pillars (Immersive, Fantasy, Stylized, Flexible)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#character-models-1)

Character Models

1.  Name bones correctly for animation
    
2.  Use 64px density
    
3.  Disable side shadows in Blockbench
    
4.  Keep proportions cartoony and bulky
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#common-mistakes-to-avoid)

Common Mistakes to Avoid


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

❌ **Using too many triangles** - Impacts performance significantly ❌ **Pure white/black colors** - Breaks in-game lighting ❌ **Stretching beyond 0.7X-1.3X** - Obvious pixel distortion ❌ **Wrong texture density** - Inconsistent with game style ❌ **Complex topology** - Keep it simple with cubes and quads ❌ **Flat, noisy textures** - Add volume and avoid grain ❌ **Spheres** - Not supported!

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#learning-resources)

Learning Resources


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#official)

Official

*   **Blockbench Plugin** - Essential tool
    
*   **Model Examples** - Download from official site
    
*   **Tutorial Videos** - Art Director's workflow
    
*   **Official Blog** - Latest art direction updates
    

###

Getting Started Checklist


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Download Blockbench
    
*   Install Hytale Blockbench Plugin
    
*   Download official model examples
    
*   Study art pillars
    
*   Practice with simple models
    
*   Choose correct texture density
    
*   Keep geometry simple (cubes and quads only)
    
*   Avoid pure white and black
    
*   Test stretching limits
    
*   Share with community for feedback

# Bootstrap/Early Plugins | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Bootstrap/Early Pluginsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:01 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#important-warning)

Important Warning


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Bootstrap/Early Plugins should only be used when absolutely necessary!**

Early plugins run during a critical phase of the loading process and can significantly impact the game's stability and behavior. Most plugins do NOT need to be early plugins.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bootstrap/Early Plugins are a special type of plugin that executes **before** the main Hytale server starts. Their primary function is low-level modification, specifically performing **class transformations** that involve altering or injecting bytecode into classes as they are loaded.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#what-are-early-plugins)

What are Early Plugins?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#key-characteristics)

Key Characteristics:

*   **Execute before main server:** Load during game initialization
    
*   **Outside standard plugin environment:** Cannot access regular plugin APIs
    
*   **No access to:** Event buses, registries, or lifecycle callbacks
    
*   **Primary purpose:** Class transformation and bytecode manipulation
    
*   **High risk:** Can cause stability issues if implemented incorrectly
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#when-to-use-early-plugins)

When to Use Early Plugins:

**Use early plugins for:**

*   Bytecode transformation/modification
    
*   Low-level core game modifications
    
*   Injecting code into existing classes
    
*   Changing fundamental game behavior
    

âŒ **Do NOT use early plugins for:**

*   Adding new items, blocks, or mobs (use Packs instead)
    
*   Implementing game features (use regular Plugins)
    
*   Listening to events (use regular Plugins)
    
*   Configuration management (use regular Plugins)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#loading-early-plugins)

Loading Early Plugins


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#default-location)

Default Location:

By default, the game loads early plugins from:

Copy

    earlyplugins/

**Important:** You must create this folder manually - the server does not create it automatically.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#custom-locations)

Custom Locations:

Additional paths can be defined using the `--early-plugins` launch argument:

Copy

    --early-plugins="C:/path/to/custom/earlyplugins"

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#user-warning-system)

User Warning System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#warning-message)

Warning Message:

When launching with early plugins installed, users see:

Copy

    ===========================================================================
                        Loaded 2 class transformer(s)!!
    ===========================================================================
                 This is unsupported and may cause stability issues.
                               Use at your own risk!!
    ===========================================================================
    Press ENTER to accept and continue...

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#skipping-the-warning)

Skipping the Warning:

*   **Manual skip:** Press ENTER key
    
*   **Auto-skip:** Add `--accept-early-plugins` launch argument
    
*   **Singleplayer:** Warning is NOT displayed
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#creating-early-plugins)

Creating Early Plugins


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#basic-requirements)

Basic Requirements:

*   Any `.jar` file can be loaded as an early plugin
    
*   **No manifest.json required**
    
*   **No standard entrypoints needed**
    
*   Must implement class transformers via service loader
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#class-transformers)

Class Transformers


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Class transformers allow you to modify the bytecode of classes as they are loaded.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#how-they-work)

How They Work:

1.  Game starts loading classes
    
2.  Before a class is loaded into the JVM
    
3.  Bytes are passed through transformer chain
    
4.  Your transformer modifies the bytes
    
5.  Modified bytes are loaded by JVM
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#step-1-registration)

Step 1: Registration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Class transformers are loaded using the **Service Loader** pattern:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#id-1.1-create-transformer-class)

1.1 Create Transformer Class:

Copy

    package com.example.early;
    
    import com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.ClassTransformer;
    
    public class ExampleTransformer implements ClassTransformer {
        
        @Override
        public byte[] transform(String name, String path, byte[] bytes) {
            // Transformation logic here
            return bytes;
        }
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#id-1.2-create-service-loader-file)

1.2 Create Service Loader File:

**Path:** `src/main/resources/META-INF/services/com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.ClassTransformer`

**Contents:**

Copy

    com.example.early.ExampleTransformer

Add the full qualified name of your transformer class to this file.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#step-2-transformer-priority)

Step 2: Transformer Priority


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transformers are executed in priority order:

*   **Higher priority** runs BEFORE lower priority
    
*   **Default priority:** 0
    
*   **Negative numbers:** Run later
    
*   **Positive numbers:** Run earlier
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#setting-priority)

Setting Priority:

Copy

    @Override
    public int priority() {
        return -100;  // Run after most other transformers
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#priority-examples)

Priority Examples:

*   `100` - Very early (runs first)
    
*   `10` - Early
    
*   `0` - Default (most transformers)
    
*   `-10` - Late
    
*   `-100` - Very late (runs last)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#step-3-restricted-classes)

Step 3: Restricted Classes


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For safety reasons, transformers **cannot modify** classes from certain packages:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#restricted-packages)

Restricted Packages:

*   `java.*`
    
*   `javax.*`
    
*   `jdk.*`
    
*   `sun.*`
    
*   `com.sun.*`
    
*   `org.bouncycastle.*`
    
*   `io.netty.*`
    
*   `org.objectweb.asm.*`
    
*   `com.google.gson.*`
    
*   `org.slf4j.*`
    
*   `org.apache.logging.*`
    
*   `ch.qos.logback.*`
    
*   `com.google.flogger.*`
    
*   `io.sentry.*`
    
*   `com.hypixel.protoplus.*`
    
*   `com.hypixel.fastutil.*`
    
*   `com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.*`
    

Attempting to transform these will be ignored or cause errors.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#step-4-writing-transformers)

Step 4: Writing Transformers


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#transform-method)

Transform Method:

Copy

    @Override
    public byte[] transform(String name, String path, byte[] bytes) {
        // name: Fully qualified class name (e.g., "com.hypixel.hytale.server.HytaleServer")
        // path: File path to the class
        // bytes: Original class bytecode
        
        // Return modified bytes, or original bytes if no changes
        return bytes;
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#basic-transformation-pattern)

Basic Transformation Pattern:

Copy

    @Override
    public byte[] transform(String name, String path, byte[] bytes) {
        // Only transform specific class
        if (name.equals("com.hypixel.hytale.server.core.HytaleServer")) {
            // Modify the bytes
            return modifyBytes(bytes);
        }
        
        // Return unchanged for other classes
        return bytes;
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#example-simple-string-replacement-transformer)

Example: Simple String Replacement Transformer


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This example replaces the startup message with a custom one:

Copy

    import com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.ClassTransformer;
    import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
    import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
    
    public class ExampleTransformer implements ClassTransformer {
    
        @Override
        public byte[] transform(String name, String path, byte[] bytes) {
            if (name.equals("com.hypixel.hytale.server.core.HytaleServer")) {
                return patchString(bytes, 
                    "Starting HytaleServer", 
                    "Starting Patched HytaleServer >:)");
            }
            return bytes;
        }
    
        /**
         * Replaces the first occurrence of a string within an array of Java class bytes.
         *
         * @param bytes       The Java class bytes.
         * @param target      The target string to be replaced.
         * @param replacement The string to replace it with.
         * @return The patched class bytes.
         */
        public static byte[] patchString(byte[] bytes, String target, String replacement) {
            final byte[] targetBytes = encodeStringWithLength(target);
            final byte[] replacementBytes = encodeStringWithLength(replacement);
            final int index = indexOf(bytes, targetBytes);
            
            if (index == -1) {
                return bytes;  // Target not found
            }
            
            final byte[] result = new byte[bytes.length - targetBytes.length + replacementBytes.length];
            System.arraycopy(bytes, 0, result, 0, index); // Before the target
            System.arraycopy(replacementBytes, 0, result, index, replacementBytes.length); // Replacement
            System.arraycopy(bytes, index + targetBytes.length, result, index + replacementBytes.length, 
                bytes.length - index - targetBytes.length); // After the target
            
            return result;
        }
    
        /**
         * Encodes a string as length (short) + UTF_8, 
         * this is the format used in Java bytecode for string constants.
         *
         * @param str The string to encode.
         * @return The encoded string.
         */
        public static byte[] encodeStringWithLength(String str) {
            final byte[] utf8Bytes = str.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
            ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(2 + utf8Bytes.length);
            return buffer.putShort((short) utf8Bytes.length).put(utf8Bytes).array();
        }
    
        /**
         * Finds the first index of a byte array within a larger sequence of bytes.
         *
         * @param array  The sequence of bytes to search through.
         * @param target The target to find.
         * @return The index of the target, or -1 if the target was not found.
         */
        private static int indexOf(byte[] array, byte[] target) {
            outer:
            for (int i = 0; i <= array.length - target.length; i++) {
                for (int j = 0; j < target.length; j++) {
                    if (array[i + j] != target[j]) {
                        continue outer;
                    }
                }
                return i;
            }
            return -1;
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#advanced-using-asm-library)

Advanced: Using ASM Library


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For more complex transformations, use the **ASM library**:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#asm-benefits)

ASM Benefits:

*   Structured bytecode manipulation
    
*   Visitor pattern for class modification
    
*   Less error-prone than raw byte manipulation
    
*   Better maintainability
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#example-asm-transformer)

Example ASM Transformer:

Copy

    import com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.ClassTransformer;
    import org.objectweb.asm.*;
    
    public class AsmTransformer implements ClassTransformer {
    
        @Override
        public byte[] transform(String name, String path, byte[] bytes) {
            if (name.equals("com.example.TargetClass")) {
                ClassReader reader = new ClassReader(bytes);
                ClassWriter writer = new ClassWriter(reader, 0);
                ClassVisitor visitor = new MyClassVisitor(Opcodes.ASM9, writer);
                reader.accept(visitor, 0);
                return writer.toByteArray();
            }
            return bytes;
        }
        
        private static class MyClassVisitor extends ClassVisitor {
            public MyClassVisitor(int api, ClassVisitor cv) {
                super(api, cv);
            }
            
            @Override
            public MethodVisitor visitMethod(int access, String name, 
                    String descriptor, String signature, String[] exceptions) {
                MethodVisitor mv = super.visitMethod(access, name, descriptor, signature, exceptions);
                
                // Modify specific method
                if (name.equals("targetMethod")) {
                    return new MethodModifier(api, mv);
                }
                
                return mv;
            }
        }
        
        private static class MethodModifier extends MethodVisitor {
            public MethodModifier(int api, MethodVisitor mv) {
                super(api, mv);
            }
            
            @Override
            public void visitCode() {
                // Inject code at method start
                super.visitCode();
                // Add your bytecode instructions here
            }
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#project-structure)

Project Structure


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    your-early-plugin/
    ├── src/
    │   └── main/
    │       ├── java/
    │       │   └── com/
    │       │       └── example/
    │       │           └── early/
    │       │               └── ExampleTransformer.java
    │       └── resources/
    │           └── META-INF/
    │               └── services/
    │                   └── com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.ClassTransformer
    ├── build.gradle
    └── README.md

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#building-early-plugins)

Building Early Plugins


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Gradle to build:

Copy

    plugins {
        id 'java'
    }
    
    group = 'com.example'
    version = '1.0.0'
    
    repositories {
        mavenCentral()
    }
    
    dependencies {
        // Add Hytale early plugin API
        compileOnly 'com.hypixel.hytale:early-plugin-api:VERSION'
        
        // ASM for bytecode manipulation (optional)
        implementation 'org.ow2.asm:asm:9.5'
        implementation 'org.ow2.asm:asm-commons:9.5'
    }
    
    jar {
        from {
            configurations.runtimeClasspath.collect { 
                it.isDirectory() ? it : zipTree(it) 
            }
        }
    }

Build command:

Copy

    ./gradlew build

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#testing-early-plugins)

Testing Early Plugins


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#id-1.-build-plugin-jar)

1\. Build Plugin JAR

Copy

    ./gradlew build

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#id-2.-copy-to-early-plugins-folder)

2\. Copy to Early Plugins Folder

Copy

    cp build/libs/your-plugin.jar /path/to/hytale/earlyplugins/

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#id-3.-launch-hytale)

3\. Launch Hytale

Copy

    # With warning
    java -jar HytaleServer.jar
    
    # Skip warning
    java -jar HytaleServer.jar --accept-early-plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#id-4.-check-logs)

4\. Check Logs

Look for:

*   "Loaded X class transformer(s)" message
    
*   Your transformer being listed
    
*   No errors during class loading
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#debugging-tips)

Debugging Tips


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#add-logging)

Add Logging:

Copy

    @Override
    public byte[] transform(String name, String path, byte[] bytes) {
        if (name.equals("target.Class")) {
            System.out.println("Transforming: " + name);
            // Transform logic
            System.out.println("Transform complete!");
        }
        return bytes;
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#check-transformer-is-loaded)

Check Transformer is Loaded:

The startup message shows how many transformers loaded:

Copy

    Loaded 2 class transformer(s)!!

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#verify-bytecode-changes)

Verify Bytecode Changes:

Use a Java decompiler to inspect the modified classes:

*   JD-GUI
    
*   CFR
    
*   Procyon
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#common-pitfalls)

Common Pitfalls


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#a-oe-modifying-restricted-classes)

âŒ Modifying restricted classes

Copy

    // DON'T: This will be ignored
    if (name.startsWith("java.")) {
        return modifyBytes(bytes);
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#a-oe-returning-null)

âŒ Returning null

Copy

    // DON'T: This will crash
    return null;

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#always-return-valid-bytes)

Always return valid bytes

Copy

    // DO: Return original or modified bytes
    return bytes;

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#a-oe-breaking-class-structure)

âŒ Breaking class structure

Copy

    // DON'T: Corrupt the bytecode
    return new byte[]{0, 0, 0};

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#use-proper-libraries)

Use proper libraries

Copy

    // DO: Use ASM or similar tools
    ClassReader reader = new ClassReader(bytes);
    // ... proper transformation

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#best-practices)

Best Practices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Only use when necessary** - Regular plugins are sufficient for 99% of mods
    
2.  **Test thoroughly** - Early plugins can break the entire game
    
3.  **Use ASM or Mixins** - Don't manipulate raw bytes unless you're an expert
    
4.  **Document transformations** - Explain what you're modifying and why
    
5.  **Handle errors gracefully** - Return original bytes if transformation fails
    
6.  **Check compatibility** - Different game versions may have different bytecode
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#early-plugin-not-loading)

Early plugin not loading:

*   Verify JAR is in `earlyplugins/` folder
    
*   Check service loader file exists and is correct
    
*   Ensure class implements `ClassTransformer`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#game-crashes-on-startup)

Game crashes on startup:

*   Your transformer may be corrupting bytecode
    
*   Check logs for stack traces
    
*   Try removing transformer to isolate issue
    
*   Validate bytecode with ASM's `CheckClassAdapter`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#transformations-not-working)

Transformations not working:

*   Verify class name matches exactly
    
*   Check if class is in restricted packages
    
*   Ensure priority is set correctly
    
*   Add debug logging to confirm method is called
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#service-loader-file-not-found)

Service loader file not found:

*   Path must be exact: `META-INF/services/com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.early.ClassTransformer`
    
*   File must be in resources folder
    
*   File must contain full class name
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#additional-resources)

Additional Resources


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#recommended-libraries)

Recommended Libraries:

*   **ASM:** [https://asm.ow2.io/arrow-up-right](https://asm.ow2.io/)
    
*   **Mixin:** Fabric's mixin library (if available for Hytale)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#learning-resources)

Learning Resources:

*   ASM documentation
    
*   JVM bytecode specification
    
*   Java class file format documentation
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins#credits)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
