# World Generation Modding | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [The Future of World Generationarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2026/1/the-future-of-world-generation)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#introduction)

Introduction


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale's world generation system is one of the most powerful modding features available. With the V2 world generator and visual node editor, you can create custom biomes, terrain, and procedural content without writing code.

> **Official Statement:** _"Anyone can create content and modify world-gen without knowing how to code, as V2 can be edited directly in our node editor."_ - Dan (World Generation Engineer)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#world-generator-versions)

World Generator Versions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#v1-current-exploration-mode)

V1 (Current - Exploration Mode)

*   **Development:** 2016-2020
    
*   **Status:** Available at Early Access launch
    
*   **Purpose:** Prototype generator with many biomes ready
    
*   **Limitations:** Barriers when creating more zones and complex biomes
    
*   **Future:** Will eventually stop generating new chunks
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#v2-future-orbis)

V2 (Future - Orbis)

*   **Development:** Since 2021
    
*   **Status:** Under construction, accessible via Gateways
    
*   **Purpose:** Next-generation world generator
    
*   **Features:** Addresses V1 limitations, enables global design goals
    
*   **Release:** Will replace V1 once Orbis is complete
    
*   **Compatibility:** Old V1 worlds remain accessible
    

> **Note:** V2 content is currently accessible through Gateways in Exploration mode, allowing early testing.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#key-features-of-v2)

Key Features of V2


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#id-1.-pattern-scanning-system)

1\. Pattern Scanning System

The pattern scanning system allows precise control over prop placement based on environmental context.

**How It Works:**

*   Configure patterns that determine where props are placed
    
*   Search for specific block configurations (e.g., floor = empty block with solid below)
    
*   Add additional checks to gather more environmental context
    
*   Patterns are fully defined by creators
    

**Example Use Cases:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#cave-markers)

Cave Markers

*   **Dark ash trees** spawn only above caves in the deeproot biome
    
*   Pattern searches for empty blocks beneath the ground
    
*   Players learn that deeproot caves (with special resources) are found under dark ash trees
    
*   Creates "Heuristics" - deeper patterns that enhance immersion and gameplay
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#log-bridges)

Log Bridges

*   Bridges spawn across rivers by searching for two shores
    
*   Automatically placed where appropriate
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#contextual-vegetation)

Contextual Vegetation

*   Yellow mushrooms and sticks spawn around cedar tree bases
    
*   Glowing mushrooms appear only in sheltered areas
    
*   Meadows of flowers spawn in dips surrounded by trees and boulders
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#id-2.-code-mods-for-programmers)

2\. Code Mods (For Programmers)

**API Features:**

*   Implement mods that automatically work with the node editor
    
*   Plug into vanilla and other modded features
    
*   Simple, interconnected components enable strong capabilities
    
*   Seamless integration between different mods and base game
    

**Technical Benefits:**

*   **Automatic multithreading** - APIs handle threading for you
    
*   **Full read access** - Access to surrounding world context
    
*   **Simplified logic** - Focus on capabilities, not threading
    
*   **Extensibility** - Tweak, extend, and add functionality
    

> **Note:** Detailed technical documentation will be released after launch.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#id-3.-visual-node-editor-no-coding-required)

3\. Visual Node Editor (No Coding Required)

The node editor is the primary tool for creating and modifying world generation.

**Key Features:**

*   **Live-Reload:** World updates in-game as you edit
    
*   **Visual Workflow:** Build advanced procedural content by linking simple nodes
    
*   **No Coding Required:** Accessible with just tutorials and practice
    
*   **Powerful:** Bridges gap between developers and creators
    

**What You Can Control:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#terrain-shape)

Terrain Shape

*   Control each biome's terrain shape independently
    
*   High precision control
    
*   Terrain transitions blend features seamlessly between biomes
    
*   Customize terrain at biome edges for better transitions
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#material-providers)

Material Providers

*   Fully control which materials terrain is made of
    
*   Assemble Material Provider nodes with configurable rules
    
*   Access terrain context (block depth, empty space above, etc.)
    
*   Example: Grass material restricted to areas with 10+ blocks of air above
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#props-system)

Props System

*   Generate localized content (POIs, vegetation, decorations)
    
*   Precise control over placement rules and distribution
    
*   Custom procedural point grid
    
*   Customizable rules determine best placement at each point
    
*   Content from prefabs or procedural generation
    

**Editing Workflow:**

*   Each biome is a separate tile (like a jigsaw piece)
    
*   Each zone is its own tile in the world patchwork
    
*   Adding new biomes or content is straightforward
    
*   Same tools used internally by Hytale team
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#official-biomes-available)

Official Biomes Available


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**All Orbis biomes will be shared with the community!**

You'll be able to:

*   View all biomes in the node editor
    
*   Modify existing biomes
    
*   Mix official content with your own creations
    
*   Learn from professional implementations
    

**Regions Shown:**

*   **Emerald Wilds** - Plains-focused biomes
    
*   **Whisperfrost Frontier** - Taiga-focused river biomes
    
*   **Howling Sands** - Desert biomes with oases
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#experimental-feature-packs)

Experimental Feature Packs


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale developers have created experimental terrain packs to showcase possibilities:

*   **Chaotic Stacked Terrain** - Exploring vertical layering
    
*   **Underwater Caves** - Complex cave systems with bracket coral and shipwrecks
    
*   **Arches Terrain** - Natural stone arches theme
    
*   **Floating Islands** - Sky islands theme
    
*   **Procedural Rings** - Alien world with ring systems
    

> **Note:** These are experimental examples, not Adventure mode content.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#modular-asset-structure)

Modular Asset Structure


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Design Philosophy:**

*   Biomes are separate tiles in a zone puzzle
    
*   Zones are tiles in the world patchwork
    
*   Easy to add and edit terrain, props, biomes, and zones
    
*   Same tools creators use as the Hytale team
    

**Benefits:**

*   Straightforward to add new biomes
    
*   Easy to integrate prefabs
    
*   Mix and match content from different sources
    
*   Modular and flexible system
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#future-roadmap)

Future Roadmap


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#short-term-after-launch)

Short-Term (After Launch)

*   Performance improvements
    
*   Upgrading existing features
    
*   More modular and flexible asset structure
    
*   First-party tutorials and guides
    
*   In-depth systems documentation
    
*   Performance optimization best practices
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#long-term)

Long-Term

*   **Procedural Rivers and Paths** - Guide players and connect places
    
*   **Procedural Architecture** - Generate dungeons, ruins, and buildings
    
*   **Organically Growing Fauna** - Increase diversity and coherence
    
*   **Waterfalls** - Dynamic water features
    
*   **Community Feedback Integration** - Shape future based on suggestions
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#world-designer-job-roles)

World Designer Job Roles


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Exciting Opportunity:**

> **Official Announcement:** _"Following the early access release, we plan to expand our team by hiring more than 15 World Designers. These roles will be filled primarily from the community."_ - Simon (CEO)

**What This Means:**

*   New job role that hasn't existed in block games before
    
*   Artists and game designers can apply
    
*   Learn using the same tools Hytale uses internally
    
*   Community members can become professional world designers
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#getting-started-with-world-generation)

Getting Started with World Generation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   Understanding of basic Hytale modding concepts
    
*   Familiarity with the Asset Editor
    
*   Creative mindset for procedural design
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#learning-path)

Learning Path

1.  **Explore Existing Biomes** - Study official Orbis biomes in the node editor
    
2.  **Start Simple** - Create basic terrain modifications
    
3.  **Learn Patterns** - Experiment with pattern scanning for props
    
4.  **Build Complexity** - Combine multiple systems
    
5.  **Share and Iterate** - Get community feedback
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#tools-youll-use)

Tools You'll Use

*   **Hytale Node Editor** - Primary world-gen tool
    
*   **Asset Editor** - For asset configuration
    
*   **In-Game Testing** - Live-reload for instant feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#best-practices)

Best Practices


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#design-principles)

Design Principles

*   **Intentional Design** - Curated and procedural balance
    
*   **Heuristics** - Create patterns that enhance immersion
    
*   **Gameplay First** - Design always serves gameplay
    
*   **Resource Balance** - Control resource distribution
    
*   **Breadcrumbing** - Guide players to meaningful content
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#technical-considerations)

Technical Considerations

*   **Performance** - Keep generation efficient
    
*   **Modularity** - Make content easy to modify and extend
    
*   **Compatibility** - Ensure mods work with vanilla and other mods
    
*   **Testing** - Use live-reload for rapid iteration
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#community-support)

Community Support


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#official-resources)

Official Resources

*   **Tutorials** - First-party guides after launch
    
*   **Documentation** - In-depth systems documentation
    
*   **Best Practices** - Performance optimization guides
    
*   **Examples** - All official Orbis biomes available
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#community-channels)

Community Channels

*   **Discord** - [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Feedback** - Community suggestions shape the future
    
*   **Collaboration** - Share techniques and discoveries
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#important-notes)

Important Notes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#early-access-reality)

Early Access Reality

*   **Asset structure will change frequently** - Core features still being completed
    
*   **Deprecation over removal** - Features being replaced will be deprecated first
    
*   **Active development** - Systems under continuous improvement
    
*   **Support for creators** - Same support given to internal designers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#compatibility)

Compatibility

*   **V1 Worlds** - Will remain accessible after V2 launch
    
*   **Gateways** - Access V2 content during development
    
*   **Pre-release Testing** - Test Orbis before full release
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#vision-statement)

Vision Statement


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> _"This new approach to world generation will redefine the block-game genre. For the first time, artists and game designers can take full ownership of world generation, with complete control over the final result. This is a fundamental shift away from a world shaped almost solely by programmers."_ - Simon (CEO)

**Goals:**

*   Hytale feels carefully handcrafted while remaining infinitely procedural
    
*   Design always serves gameplay first
    
*   Intentionally expansive - alternate worlds, new dimensions, different spaces
    
*   Beyond Orbis - new blocks, items, prefabs, zones, regions, biomes, NPCs, quests, stories
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#next-steps)

Next Steps


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Wait for Early Access** - V2 tools will be available after launch
    
2.  **Study Official Biomes** - Learn from professional implementations
    
3.  **Join Community** - Connect with other world designers
    
4.  **Experiment** - Try creating simple modifications first
    
5.  **Share Your Work** - Contribute to the ecosystem

# Useful Tools & Links | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Official Hytale Resourcesarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page provides a curated collection of official tools, community resources, and development utilities for Hytale modding. Whether you're creating Packs, developing Plugins, or designing worlds, these resources will help streamline your workflow.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#official-hytale-tools)

Official Hytale Tools


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#blockbench--hytale-plugin)

Blockbench + Hytale Plugin ⭐

**Website:** [https://www.blockbench.netarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/)
 **Hytale Plugin:** [https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale\_pluginarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale_plugin)
 **Plugin Source:** [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/JannisX11/hytale-blockbench-plugin)
 **Official Guide:** [Making Models for Hytalearrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/12/an-introduction-to-making-models-for-hytale)

**Description:** The **officially supported** tool for creating Hytale models, textures, and animations. Replaces Hytale's internal modeling tools to support established creative workflows.

**Status:** Releasing soon (Early Access)

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features)

Features:

*   Create Hytale-compatible models, textures, and animations
    
*   Maintains consistent pixel ratio across textures
    
*   Exports in correct Hytale format
    
*   Quality-of-life improvements for Hytale workflow
    
*   Texture painting and UV mapping
    
*   Real-time preview
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#official-art-style-guidelines)

Official Art Style Guidelines:

*   **Primitives:** Only cubes and quads (no spheres!)
    
*   **Texture Density:** 64px/unit for characters, 32px/unit for props/blocks
    
*   **Texture Size:** Multiples of 32px (32, 64, 96, 128, etc.)
    
*   **Stretching Limits:** 0.7X to 1.3X on any axis
    
*   **Colors:** Avoid pure white and pure black
    
*   **Triangle Count:** Keep optimized for performance
    

**Official Models:** [Download Examplesarrow-up-right](https://cdn.hytale.com/Hytale%20Model%20Examples.zip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#getting-started)

Getting Started:

1.  Download Blockbench from the official website
    
2.  Install the Hytale Blockbench plugin
    
3.  Study official model examples
    
4.  Follow [Blockbench Modeling Guide](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide)
    
5.  Export in Hytale format
    
6.  Place files in your Pack's `Common/` folder
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#file-formats)

File Formats:

*   **Models:** `.blockymodel` - Custom block/item models
    
*   **Animations:** `.blockyanim` - Block animation files
    
*   **Textures:** `.png` - Standard PNG images (multiples of 32px)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#hytale-asset-editor)

Hytale Asset Editor

**Access:** Built into Hytale (Creation Tools tab) **Official Info:** [Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

**Description:** Visual editor for data assets (JSON files). Supports most asset types with some limitations.

**Status:** Available now in Early Access

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features-1)

Features:

*   Edit data assets visually (no coding required)
    
*   Supports blocks, items, and most asset types
    
*   Direct integration with Hytale
    
*   Live preview of changes
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#current-limitations)

Current Limitations:

*   Notable limitations around NPCs
    
*   World generation editing limited
    
*   Interactions not fully exposed
    
*   **Note:** Will expand over time
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#use-cases)

Use Cases:

*   Modify block properties
    
*   Configure item behaviors
    
*   Edit asset metadata
    
*   Visual asset configuration
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#asset-graph-editor-node-editor)

Asset Graph Editor (Node Editor)

**Access:** Built into Hytale (after launch) **Official Info:** [World Generation Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2026/1/the-future-of-world-generation)

**Description:** Node-based editor for complex assets like world generation, NPCs, and creative tool brushes.

**Status:** Currently being released

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features-2)

Features:

*   Visual node-graph interface
    
*   Live-reload in-game
    
*   No coding required
    
*   Build advanced procedural content by linking simple nodes
    
*   Full control over biomes, terrain, props, and materials
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#use-cases-1)

Use Cases:

*   World generation (biomes, terrain, props)
    
*   NPC behavior configuration
    
*   Creative tool brush creation
    
*   Complex asset configuration
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#world-generation-capabilities)

World Generation Capabilities:

*   **Pattern Scanning System** - Contextual prop placement
    
*   **Terrain Shape Control** - Independent biome terrain
    
*   **Material Providers** - Control terrain materials
    
*   **Props System** - POIs, vegetation, decorations
    
*   **Live-Reload** - Instant in-game feedback
    

**Note:** Internal tool being made public - expect rough edges but useful functionality.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#creative-mode-tools)

Creative Mode Tools

**Access:** Built into Hytale (Creative Mode) **Official Info:** [Creative Mode Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-creative-mode)

**Description:** Interactive suite of in-game tools for world editing and content creation.

**Status:** Available in Early Access

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#tools-available)

Tools Available:

*   **Scripted Brushes** - Asset-defined brushes (mountains, paths, ruins)
    
*   **Shape Brush** - Paint pyramids, cones, squares, and more
    
*   **Selection Tool** - 3D selections, copy, paste, move, rotate
    
*   **Paste Tool** - Precise prefab placement
    
*   **Ruler Tool** - Measure distances and mark outlines
    
*   **Laser Pointer** - Point out locations to friends
    
*   **Machinima Tool** - Camera animation and recording
    
*   **Prefab Browser/Editor** - Browse and edit prefabs
    
*   **Player Model Changer** - Become any NPC model
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#creative-mode-features)

Creative Mode Features:

*   Customizable flight (speed, controls, inertia)
    
*   Quick Settings Panel
    
*   Help Menu for commands
    
*   Real-time world modification
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#machinima-tools)

Machinima Tools

**Access:** Built into Hytale **Official Info:** [Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

**Description:** Tools used to create the official 2018 Hytale trailer. Create cinematic content with camera animations.

**Status:** Available but needs technical fixes

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features-3)

Features:

*   Camera actor placement
    
*   Keyframe animation
    
*   Speed and timing control
    
*   Cinematic recording
    

**Note:** Scheduled for massive upgrade in functionality and UX after launch.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#community-resources)

Community Resources


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#hytaleguide.net)

HytaleGuide.net ⭐

**Website:** [https://hytaleguide.netarrow-up-right](https://hytaleguide.net/)
 **Forum:** [Community Forumarrow-up-right](https://hytaleguide.net/)

**Description:** Comprehensive wiki dedicated to Hytale gameplay content, items, mobs, zones, and adventure mode information.

**Content:**

*   **Items Database** - Weapons, armor, food, and item stats
    
*   **Mobs Encyclopedia** - Creature information, drops, and locations
    
*   **Zones Guide** - Emerald Grove, Borea, Devastated Lands, Howling Sands
    
*   **Biomes Information** - Biome-specific content and features
    
*   **Alterverses** - Information about Orbis and other planets
    
*   **Guides Section** - Gameplay guides and tutorials
    
*   **Community Forum** - Discussion and server listings
    

**Perfect for:**

*   Learning about Hytale gameplay content
    
*   Understanding items, mobs, and zones
    
*   Adventure mode information
    
*   Community discussions and server listings
    

**Note:** Focuses on gameplay content rather than modding - complementary to modding documentation.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#hytale-modding-documentation)

Hytale Modding Documentation

**Website:** [https://hytalemodding.devarrow-up-right](https://hytalemodding.dev/en/docs)
 **GitHub:** [HytaleModding/sitearrow-up-right](https://github.com/HytaleModding/site)

**Description:** Community-driven documentation site providing comprehensive guides and resources for Hytale modding. Open source and accepting contributions.

**Content:**

*   **Quick Start** - Setting up a standard Hytale project
    
*   **Learning to Learn** - Meta-learning guide for becoming a better learner
    
*   **3D Modeling Guides** - Fundamentals, techniques, and best practices
    
*   **Java Basics Series** - Programming tutorials for beginners
    
*   **Publishing Your Mod** - How to distribute mods
    
*   **Established Information** - Core modding concepts and FAQ
    
*   **Contributing** - How to contribute to their documentation
    

**Philosophy:**

> "It is important to note that modding Hytale is not restricted to programming plugins. Programming, visual scripting, texturing, 3D modelling, modifying assets, etc. are all modding. In Hytale, anyone can be a modder."

**Perfect for:**

*   Beginners learning Java programming
    
*   Those looking for community-driven tutorials
    
*   Modders wanting to publish their work
    
*   Contributors who want to help improve documentation
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#hytale-modding-video-tutorials)

Hytale Modding Video Tutorials

**YouTube Playlist:** [Modding by Kaupenjoearrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLKGarocXCE1EBIOx2UTpGPZyWMpanSnDj)

**Description:** Comprehensive video tutorial series covering Hytale modding from basics to advanced topics.

**Content:**

*   Step-by-step video guides
    
*   Visual demonstrations
    
*   Practical examples
    
*   Beginner-friendly explanations
    
*   Advanced techniques and patterns
    

**Perfect for:** Visual learners who prefer video tutorials over written documentation.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#development-tools)

Development Tools


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#intellij-idea)

IntelliJ IDEA

**Website:** [https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/arrow-up-right](https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/)

**Description:** The recommended IDE for Java plugin development.

**Versions:**

*   **Community Edition:** Free, sufficient for Hytale plugin development
    
*   **Ultimate Edition:** Paid, includes additional features
    

**Why IntelliJ:**

*   Excellent Java support
    
*   Built-in Gradle integration
    
*   Powerful debugging tools
    
*   Code completion and refactoring
    
*   Integration with version control
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#java-development-kit-jdk)

Java Development Kit (JDK)

**Required Version:** Java 25

**Download:**

*   **Oracle JDK:** [https://www.oracle.com/java/arrow-up-right](https://www.oracle.com/java/)
    
*   **OpenJDK:** [https://openjdk.org/arrow-up-right](https://openjdk.org/)
    

**Note:** Hytale plugins require Java 25 specifically.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#gradle)

Gradle

**Website:** [https://gradle.org/arrow-up-right](https://gradle.org/)

**Description:** Build automation tool used for compiling and packaging Hytale plugins.

**Features:**

*   Dependency management
    
*   Build automation
    
*   Plugin packaging
    
*   Task execution
    

**Note:** Usually included with plugin templates, manual installation not typically required.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#custom-gradle-plugin-for-server-testing)

Custom Gradle Plugin for Server Testing

**Documentation:** [Gradle Automation & Testing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/13-gradle-automation-testing)

**Description:** Custom Gradle plugin that automates the entire development workflow: build, deploy, and test your plugin on a Hytale server with a single command.

**Features:**

*   Automatic server JAR download and caching
    
*   Compiles and deploys your plugin automatically
    
*   Starts server with interactive console
    
*   One-command workflow: `./gradlew runServer`
    
*   Saves hours of manual testing time
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Rapid plugin development and testing
    
*   Automated CI/CD pipelines
    
*   Multi-version server testing
    
*   Remote debugging support
    

**Learn More:** See the complete implementation guide in [Gradle Automation & Testing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/13-gradle-automation-testing)
.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#graphics-and-design-tools)

Graphics & Design Tools

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#paint.net)

Paint.NET

**Website:** [https://www.getpaint.net/arrow-up-right](https://www.getpaint.net/)

**Description:** Free image editing software for Windows, perfect for creating textures.

**Use Cases:**

*   Creating block textures (16x16, 32x32)
    
*   Editing icons
    
*   Creating UI elements
    
*   Alpha channel support

GIMP

**Website:** [https://www.gimp.org/arrow-up-right](https://www.gimp.org/)

**Description:** Free and open-source image editor, available for all platforms.

**Use Cases:**

*   Advanced texture creation
    
*   Photo manipulation
    
*   Complex transparency effects
    
*   Texture atlases

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#version-control)

Version Control


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#git)

Git

**Website:** [https://git-scm.com/arrow-up-right](https://git-scm.com/)

**Description:** Version control system to track changes in your mod projects.

**Why Use Git:**

*   Track all changes to your code
    
*   Collaborate with other developers
    
*   Revert to previous versions if needed
    
*   Create branches for experimental features
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#github)

GitHub

**Website:** [https://github.com/arrow-up-right](https://github.com/)

**Description:** Online platform for hosting Git repositories.

**Benefits:**

*   Share your mods with the community
    
*   Collaborate with other modders
    
*   Issue tracking
    
*   Free for public and private repositories
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#code-libraries-and-tools)

Code Libraries & Tools


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#asm)

ASM

**Website:** [https://asm.ow2.io/arrow-up-right](https://asm.ow2.io/)

**Description:** Java bytecode manipulation and analysis framework.

**Use Cases:**

*   Creating early/bootstrap plugins
    
*   Advanced class transformations
    
*   Bytecode injection
    

**Note:** Only needed for advanced plugin development.

**Website:** [https://java-decompiler.github.io/arrow-up-right](https://java-decompiler.github.io/)
 View Java source code from `.class` files.

 Another Java decompiler with different strengths.

*   Debugging class transformations
    
*   Learning from vanilla implementations

*   [https://jsonformatter.curiousconcept.com/arrow-up-right](https://jsonformatter.curiousconcept.com/)
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Checking block/item definitions
    
*   Finding syntax errors

 **Discord:** [CurseForge UGC Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/S3EaZArYz2)

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#getting-help)

Getting Help


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#when-youre-stuck)

When You're Stuck:

1.  **Check Documentation:** Review the official tutorials first
    
2.  **Search Community Forums:** Someone may have asked your question
    
3.  **Ask the Community:** Join Hytale modding communities
    
4.  **Check Examples:** Look at vanilla assets or other mods
    
5.  **Read Error Logs:** They often contain helpful information
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#how-to-ask-good-questions)

How to Ask Good Questions:

*   Describe what you're trying to achieve
    
*   Show what you've tried
    
*   Include error messages
    
*   Provide relevant code/JSON
    
*   Mention your environment (OS, Java version, etc.)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#contributing)

Contributing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#share-your-tools)

Share Your Tools:

If you've created useful tools for Hytale modding:

1.  Share them on community forums
    
2.  Submit to the Hytale Modding Wiki
    
3.  Create GitHub repositories
    
4.  Write tutorials

Report Broken Links:

If any links in this documentation are broken or outdated:

*   Report on GitHub issues
    
*   Join community discussions
    
*   Suggest updates via pull requests

# Hytale Modding Overview | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Official Hytale Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#introduction)

Introduction


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to Hytale modding! This documentation provides comprehensive tutorials and guides for creating mods in Hytale, from asset packs to advanced Java plugins.

> **Important:** Hytale is currently in **Early Access**. The modding tools and documentation are actively being developed and improved. Expect rough edges, but also expect rapid improvements based on community feedback.

> **Official Statement:** _"We're building Hytale with modding at its core. Most of what you see in the game can be changed, extended, or removed entirely."_ - Slikey (Technical Director)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#four-official-modding-categories)

Four Official Modding Categories


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

According to [Hytale's official modding strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)
, Hytale modding falls into **four technical categories**:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-1.-server-plugins-java-.jar-files)

1\. Server Plugins (Java .jar files)

**Server Plugins** are Java-based mods that:

*   Extend the functionality of the server programmatically
    
*   Are extremely powerful and allow deep modifications to gameplay and core systems
    
*   Enable you to build minigames, economies, commands, custom logic, new asset types, and more
    
*   Require Java programming knowledge
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Custom game modes and minigames
    
*   Economy systems
    
*   Custom commands
    
*   Server management tools
    
*   Advanced gameplay mechanics
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-2.-data-assets-json-files)

2\. Data Assets (JSON files)

**Data Assets** drive gameplay behavior and define core content:

*   **Blocks and Items** - Define properties, behaviors, and interactions
    
*   **NPCs** - Configure mob behavior and AI
    
*   **World Generation** - Control terrain, biomes, and structures
    
*   **Drop Tables and Loot** - Define what items drop from blocks and mobs
    
*   **And more** - Most game content is data-driven
    

**Key Feature:** No coding required - edit JSON files to modify game content

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-3.-art-assets-sounds-models-textures)

3\. Art Assets (Sounds, Models, Textures)

**Art Assets** provide the visual and audio representation of game elements:

*   **Models** - 3D block and entity models
    
*   **Textures** - Visual appearance of blocks, items, and entities
    
*   **Sounds** - Audio effects and music
    
*   **Animations** - Movement and behavior animations
    

**Official Tool:** Blockbench is officially supported for creating Hytale models, textures, and animations

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-4.-save-files-worlds-and-prefabs)

4\. Save Files (Worlds and Prefabs)

**Save Files** allow you to share complete creations:

*   **Worlds** - Share entire playable worlds
    
*   **Prefabs** - Prebuilt structures like trees, houses, or landmarks
    
*   **Usage** - Prefabs are used in creative tools and world generation
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#important-no-text-based-scripting)

Important: No Text-Based Scripting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Clarification:** Hytale will **NOT** support text-based scripting languages like Lua.

**Why?**

*   Text-based scripting claims to "help non-programmers" but still requires programming concepts
    
*   It forces programmers to juggle two languages
    
*   It increases complexity for both designers and programmers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#instead-visual-scripting-coming-soon)

Instead: Visual Scripting (Coming Soon)

Hytale will implement **Visual Scripting** (similar to Unreal Engine Blueprints):

*   **For Designers:** Build logic visually without coding
    
*   **For Programmers:** Extend the system by creating new nodes in Java
    
*   **Sandboxed and Safe:** Visual scripts can be shared safely without security risks
    
*   **Future Vision:** Visual scripting directly in the 3D world (link levers, doors, triggers, etc.)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#modding-philosophy)

Modding Philosophy


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale's modding is built on key principles:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#server-side-first)

Server-Side First

*   All modding is server-based (both singleplayer and multiplayer)
    
*   Join any modded server without downloading external mods
    
*   No client-side mods for security and consistency
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#one-community-one-client)

One Community, One Client

*   Avoid fragmented ecosystem with different modded clients
    
*   Client remains stable, secure, and consistent
    
*   Servers provide creativity and variation
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#modding-for-longevity)

Modding for Longevity

*   Long-term commitment to modding support
    
*   Built with the same tools used to create the game
    
*   "Anything we do, you can do as well"
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#official-modding-tools)

Official Modding Tools


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale provides several official tools for creating content:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-1.-hytale-asset-editor)

1\. Hytale Asset Editor

*   **Purpose:** Editor for data assets (JSON files)
    
*   **Status:** Available now
    
*   **Capabilities:** Supports most asset types
    
*   **Limitations:** Notable limitations around NPCs, world generation, and interactions (being improved)
    
*   **Access:** Built into the game
    

![](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fs3.amazonaws.com%2Fcdn.freshdesk.com%2Fdata%2Fhelpdesk%2Fattachments%2Fproduction%2F9242437642%2Foriginal%2FfG1dqRJeDvDzMh_XoZ6vSgTB_iYSUtTRKA.png%3F1767794173&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b2b5d9a&sv=2)

Asset Editor

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-2.-blockbench-plugin)

2\. Blockbench Plugin

*   **Purpose:** Create Hytale-compatible models, textures, and animations
    
*   **Status:** Releasing soon
    
*   **Integration:** Direct integration with Blockbench
    
*   **Replaces:** Hytale's own internal modeling tools
    
*   **Why:** Better support for established creative workflows in the community
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-3.-asset-graph-editor)

3\. Asset Graph Editor

*   **Purpose:** Node-based editor for complex assets
    
*   **Status:** Currently being released
    
*   **Use Cases:** World generation, creative tool brushes, NPCs
    
*   **Note:** Internal tool being made public - expect rough edges but useful functionality
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-4.-creative-mode-tools)

4\. Creative Mode Tools

*   **Purpose:** Interactive suite of in-game world editing and creation tools
    
*   **Status:** Available in Early Access
    
*   **Access:** Switch to Creative Mode in any world
    
*   **Official Info:** [Creative Mode Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-creative-mode)
    

**Available Tools:**

*   **Scripted Brushes** - Create mountains, paths, procedural ruins (asset-defined, modder-creatable)
    
*   **Shape Brush** - Paint pyramids, cones, squares with customizable size, density, materials
    
*   **Selection Tool** - 3D selections, copy, paste, move, rotate, save prefabs, regenerate chunks
    
*   **Paste Tool** - Precise prefab placement with arrow key controls
    
*   **Ruler/Laser Pointer** - Measure distances and point out locations
    
*   **Prefab Browser/Editor** - Browse 100+ models, edit in separate environment
    
*   **Player Model Changer** - Become any NPC model
    
*   **Machinima Camera** - Keyframe animation for cinematic recording
    

**Creative Mode Features:**

*   Customizable flight (speed, controls, hover/directional, inertia)
    
*   Quick Settings Panel (changes based on tool in hand)
    
*   Help Menu for quick command discovery
    
*   Real-time world modification with instant feedback
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-5.-machinima-tools)

5\. Machinima Tools

*   **Purpose:** Create cinematic content (used for the 2018 trailer)
    
*   **Status:** Available but needs technical fixes
    
*   **Quality:** Delivered great results for official trailers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#id-6.-custom-ui-framework-noesisgui)

6\. Custom UI Framework (NoesisGUI)

*   **Purpose:** Create custom user interfaces
    
*   **Status:** In transition - consolidating from 3 UI frameworks to 1
    
*   **Framework:** NoesisGUI (official UI framework)
    
*   **Current State:** Asset-driven UIs are available but incomplete
    
*   **Recommendation:** Start experimenting and provide feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#official-documentation-and-resources)

Official Documentation & Resources


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#official-hytale-documentation-gitbook)

Official Hytale Documentation (GitBook)

*   **Status:** In progress
    
*   **Platform:** GitBook (same as this documentation!)
    
*   **Note:** Will start incomplete but expand based on community questions
    
*   **Official Statement:** _"We are working on public creator documentation hosted on GitBook"_
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#server-source-code-coming-soon)

Server Source Code (Coming Soon)

*   **Release:** Within 1-2 months after Early Access launch (March 2026)
    
*   **Access:** Full server source code will be shared
    
*   **Purpose:**
    
    *   Inspect how systems work under the hood
        
    *   Unblock yourself when documentation is incomplete
        
    *   Contribute improvements and bug fixes
        
    
*   **Note:** Server is not obfuscated - can be decompiled now
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#development-bounties-future)

Development Bounties (Future)

*   **Plan:** Open bounties for specific improvements and features
    
*   **Goal:** Reward contributions that strengthen the ecosystem
    
*   **Timeline:** Takes time to set up properly
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#community-and-support)

Community & Support


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#official-channels)

Official Channels

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
     - Talk directly with developers and modders
    
*   **Discord (CurseForge):** [CurseForge UGC Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/S3EaZArYz2)
     - User-generated content focus
    
*   **X / Reddit:** Tweet at @Hytale or post on Hytale subreddits
    
*   **Official Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
     - Latest updates and strategy posts
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#what-to-expect)

What to Expect

*   **Early Access Reality:** Tools are uneven, documentation is incomplete, some workflows are frustrating
    
*   **Rapid Improvements:** Developers are fixing issues as they come in
    
*   **Transparency:** Developers commit to being honest about what's ready and what's not
    
*   **Your Feedback Matters:** Hold developers accountable, demand answers, provide feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#important-warnings)

Important Warnings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#data-safety)

Data Safety

> **Critical:** Hytale is in true Early Access. There are crashes, and some can cause **data loss**.

**Practical Advice:**

*   **Take frequent backups** of your savegames and creations
    
*   Treat this phase as valuable but **not yet safe for irreplaceable work**
    
*   Automatic backup solutions are being developed
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#current-limitations)

Current Limitations

*   Missing editing capabilities for some features
    
*   Client behavior not fully exposed to server
    
*   Some tools are rough, inconsistent, or painful to work with
    
*   Modding maturity varies wildly depending on what you're building
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#long-term-vision)

Long-Term Vision


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#node-editors-coming)

Node Editors (Coming)

*   **Purpose:** Visual editors for complex JSON assets
    
*   **Target:** NPCs, Interactions, World Generation
    
*   **Integration:** Directly into Hytale Asset Editor
    
*   **Goal:** Unified creator suite instead of patchwork tools
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#visual-scripting-core-pillar)

Visual Scripting (Core Pillar)

*   **Timeline:** Long-term priority
    
*   **Features:**
    
    *   Sandboxed, safe environment for sharing logic
        
    *   Great learnability for all skill levels
        
    *   Programmers can extend with performance-critical nodes
        
    *   Eventually: Visual scripting directly in the 3D world
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#first-party-server-network)

First-Party Server Network

*   **Plan:** Hypixel-style minigames network
    
*   **Purpose:**
    
    *   Validate modding tools at scale
        
    *   Share code and assets for learning
        
    *   Ensure playable content during early days
        
    
*   **Note:** Not trying to compete with community servers
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#getting-started)

Getting Started


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#for-content-creators-no-coding)

For Content Creators (No Coding)

1.  Start with **Packs** - Create blocks, items, and content using JSON
    
2.  Use the **Asset Editor** to modify properties visually
    
3.  Learn **Blockbench** for custom models and textures
    
4.  Follow the [Getting Started with Packs](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs)
     guide
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#for-developers-java)

For Developers (Java)

1.  Learn **Java programming** fundamentals
    
2.  Set up your development environment (IntelliJ IDEA recommended)
    
3.  Clone the [Plugin Templatearrow-up-right](https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin)
    
4.  Follow the [Getting Started with Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/07-getting-started-with-plugins)
     guide
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#for-advanced-users)

For Advanced Users

1.  Explore **Bootstrap/Early Plugins** for low-level modifications
    
2.  Study the decompiled server source (or wait for official release)
    
3.  Follow the [Bootstrap/Early Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins)
     guide
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started#closing-words)

Closing Words


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_From Slikey (Technical Director):_

# Getting Started with Plugins | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Getting Started with Pluginsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:09 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide will help you get started with creating **Plugins** for Hytale. Plugins are mods written in **Java** that use the game's API to expand vanilla functionality and add new content programmatically.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you begin, ensure you have:

*   **Hytale** installed via the official launcher
    
*   **IntelliJ IDEA** (Community Edition is fine)
    
*   **Java 25** downloaded and configured
    
*   Basic **Java programming** knowledge
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-1-download-the-idea-template)

Step 1: Download the IDEA Template


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The easiest way to start developing plugins is by using the official template created by **Darkhax & Jared**.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#download-options)

Download Options:

*   **Zip File:** (Link TBC - Check Community documentation)
    
*   **GitHub Repo:** (Link TBC - Check Community documentation)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#template-features)

Template Features:

The template includes many great features:

*   Adds the latest Hytale server files to your classpath
    
*   Run the game from your IDE with breakpoint support
    
*   Bundle assets with your plugin (editable with in-game Asset Editor)
    
*   Supports various patch lines (releases and pre-releases)
    
*   Includes example code and assets
    
*   Pre-configured Gradle build system
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-2-setup-the-template)

Step 2: Setup the Template


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-2.1-extract-the-template)

2.1 Extract the Template

1.  Download the ZIP file
    
2.  Extract contents to your desired development location
    
3.  Read the included `README.md` for detailed setup instructions
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-2.2-complete-prerequisites-checklist)

2.2 Complete Prerequisites Checklist

Ensure you have completed all the following before proceeding:

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#prerequisites-checklist)

Prerequisites Checklist:

1.  **Download Hytale** using the official launcher
    
2.  **Install IntelliJ IDEA** (Community Edition is sufficient)
    
3.  **Download Java 25** and add it as an SDK in IDEA
    
4.  **Set your project name** in `settings.gradle`
    
5.  **Review the properties** in `gradle.properties`
    
6.  **Update the manifest** in `src/main/resources/manifest.json`
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-3-configure-your-project)

Step 3: Configure Your Project


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-3.1-set-project-name)

3.1 Set Project Name

Edit `settings.gradle`:

Copy

    rootProject.name = 'your-plugin-name'

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-3.2-review-gradle-properties)

3.2 Review Gradle Properties

Open and review `gradle.properties`:

Copy

    # Example properties (actual values may vary)
    hytale_version=latest
    plugin_version=1.0.0
    # ... other properties

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-3.3-update-manifest-file)

3.3 Update Manifest File

Edit `src/main/resources/manifest.json` with your project information:

Copy

    {
      "Group": "com.yourname",
      "Name": "YourPluginName",
      "Version": "1.0.0",
      "Description": "Description of your plugin",
      "Authors": [\
        {\
          "Name": "Your Name",\
          "Email": "your.email@example.com",\
          "Url": "https://your-website.com"\
        }\
      ],
      "Website": "https://your-plugin-website.com",
      "ServerVersion": "*",
      "Dependencies": {},
      "OptionalDependencies": {},
      "DisabledByDefault": false
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-4-open-the-project-in-idea)

Step 4: Open the Project in IDEA


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Launch IntelliJ IDEA**
    
2.  **Open Project:**
    
    *   Click `File` –†’ `Open`
        
    *   Navigate to your extracted template folder
        
    *   Select the folder and click `OK`
        
    
3.  **Wait for Initialization:**
    
    *   IDEA will import the Gradle project
        
    *   Dependencies will be downloaded automatically
        
    *   This may take several minutes on first run
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-5-configure-java-25-sdk)

Step 5: Configure Java 25 SDK


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you haven't already added Java 25 as an SDK:

1.  **Open Project Structure:**
    
    *   `File` –†’ `Project Structure` (or `Ctrl+Alt+Shift+S`)
        
    
2.  **Add SDK:**
    
    *   Click `SDKs` under `Platform Settings`
        
    *   Click `+` –†’ `Add JDK`
        
    *   Navigate to your Java 25 installation
        
    *   Click `OK`
        
    
3.  **Set Project SDK:**
    
    *   Go to `Project` settings
        
    *   Set `SDK` to Java 25
        
    *   Click `Apply` and `OK`
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-6-understanding-the-project-structure)

Step 6: Understanding the Project Structure


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    your-plugin-name/
    |-- src/
    |   `-- main/
    |       |-- java/
    |       |   `-- com/
    |       |       `-- yourname/
    |       |           `-- yourplugin/
    |       |               `-- YourPlugin.java
    |       `-- resources/
    |           |-- manifest.json
    |           |-- Common/          # Assets (models, textures)
    |           `-- Server/          # Server-side data
    |-- build.gradle
    |-- settings.gradle
    |-- gradle.properties
    `-- README.md

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-7-running-the-game-from-idea)

Step 7: Running the Game from IDEA


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#pre-configured-run-configuration)

Pre-configured Run Configuration

The template includes a run configuration called **HytaleServer**:

1.  **Select Run Configuration:**
    
    *   Look for the dropdown in the top-right of IDEA
        
    *   Select `HytaleServer`
        
    
2.  **Run or Debug:**
    
    *   Click the green play button to run
        
    *   Click the bug button to debug with breakpoints
        
    
3.  **Game Launches:**
    
    *   Hytale will start with your plugin loaded
        
    *   You can set breakpoints in your code
        
    *   Debug console shows plugin output
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-8-building-your-plugin)

Step 8: Building Your Plugin


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create a shareable JAR file of your plugin:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#build-with-gradle)

Build with Gradle:

**Option 1: Terminal**

Copy

    ./gradlew build

**Option 2: IDEA Gradle Panel**

1.  Open the Gradle panel (right side of IDEA)
    
2.  Navigate to: `Tasks` –†’ `build` –†’ `build`
    
3.  Double-click `build`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#output-location)

Output Location:

Your plugin JAR will be in:

Copy

    build/libs/your-plugin-name-1.0.0.jar

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#step-9-installing-plugins)

Step 9: Installing Plugins


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To install plugins in Hytale:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#installation-path)

Installation Path:

Copy

    %appdata%/Hytale/UserData/Mods/

**Full Path (Windows):**

Copy

    C:\Users\YourUsername\AppData\Roaming\Hytale\UserData\Mods\

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#installation-steps)

Installation Steps:

1.  **Create Mods Folder** (if it doesn't exist)
    
2.  **Copy your plugin JAR** into the `Mods/` folder
    
3.  **Launch Hytale**
    
4.  Your plugin will be loaded automatically
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#example-plugin-code)

Example Plugin Code


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here's a basic plugin structure:

Copy

    package com.yourname.yourplugin;
    
    import com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.JavaPlugin;
    import com.hypixel.hytale.plugin.JavaPluginInit;
    import javax.annotation.Nonnull;
    
    public class YourPlugin extends JavaPlugin {
    
        public YourPlugin(@Nonnull JavaPluginInit init) {
            super(init);
            
            // Plugin initialization code
            getLogger().info("YourPlugin has been loaded!");
        }
    
        @Override
        public void onEnable() {
            // Called when plugin is enabled
            getLogger().info("YourPlugin enabled!");
        }
    
        @Override
        public void onDisable() {
            // Called when plugin is disabled
            getLogger().info("YourPlugin disabled!");
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#plugin-development-tips)

Plugin Development Tips


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-1.-use-the-logger)

1\. Use the Logger

Copy

    getLogger().info("Information message");
    getLogger().warn("Warning message");
    getLogger().error("Error message");

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-2.-register-event-listeners)

2\. Register Event Listeners

Copy

    getServer().getPluginManager().registerEvents(new MyListener(), this);

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-3.-access-the-api)

3\. Access the API

The template includes Hytale's API in the classpath:

*   Explore the API through IntelliJ's autocomplete
    
*   Check the example code included in the template
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#id-4.-bundle-assets)

4\. Bundle Assets

You can include Packs (assets) with your Plugin:

*   Add assets to `src/main/resources/Common/` and `Server/`
    
*   They'll be bundled with your plugin JAR
    
*   Editable in-game via the Asset Editor
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#debugging-tips)

Debugging Tips


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#breakpoints)

Breakpoints

1.  Click in the left margin next to a line number
    
2.  A red dot appears indicating a breakpoint
    
3.  Run in Debug mode
    
4.  Execution pauses at breakpoints
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#console-output)

Console Output

*   Plugin logs appear in the IDEA console
    
*   Use `getLogger()` for clean output
    
*   Check for error stack traces
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#hot-reload)

Hot Reload

*   Some changes can be reloaded without restarting
    
*   Rebuild the project (`Ctrl+F9`)
    
*   Major changes require a full restart
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#next-steps)

Next Steps


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After setting up your plugin development environment:

1.  **Explore the API** - Browse available classes and methods
    
2.  **Read Example Code** - Study the included examples
    
3.  **Create Custom Features** - Start implementing your ideas
    
4.  **Use Config Files** - See "Custom Config Files" tutorial
    
5.  **Advanced Modding** - Explore "Bootstrap/Early Plugins" if needed
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#gradle-sync-fails)

Gradle sync fails:

*   Check internet connection (downloads dependencies)
    
*   Verify Java 25 is properly installed
    
*   Try: `./gradlew clean build`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#hytaleserver-run-config-missing)

HytaleServer run config missing:

*   Re-import Gradle project
    
*   Check `build.gradle` for run configuration setup
    
*   Manually create run configuration if needed
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#plugin-doesnt-load)

Plugin doesn't load:

*   Verify manifest.json is correct
    
*   Check logs for error messages
    
*   Ensure plugin JAR is in correct Mods folder
    
*   Confirm Hytale version compatibility
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#breakpoints-dont-work)

Breakpoints don't work:

*   Ensure you're running in Debug mode (bug icon)
    
*   Verify breakpoint is in executed code
    
*   Check that source code matches compiled JAR
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development#additional-resources)
