# Useful Tools & Links | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Official Hytale Resourcesarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page provides a curated collection of official tools, community resources, and development utilities for Hytale modding. Whether you're creating Packs, developing Plugins, or designing worlds, these resources will help streamline your workflow.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#official-hytale-tools)

Official Hytale Tools


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#blockbench--hytale-plugin)

Blockbench + Hytale Plugin ⭐

**Website:** [https://www.blockbench.netarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/)
 **Hytale Plugin:** [https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale\_pluginarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale_plugin)
 **Plugin Source:** [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/JannisX11/hytale-blockbench-plugin)
 **Official Guide:** [Making Models for Hytalearrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/12/an-introduction-to-making-models-for-hytale)

**Description:** The **officially supported** tool for creating Hytale models, textures, and animations. Replaces Hytale's internal modeling tools to support established creative workflows.

**Status:** Releasing soon (Early Access)

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#features)

Features:

*   Create Hytale-compatible models, textures, and animations
    
*   Maintains consistent pixel ratio across textures
    
*   Exports in correct Hytale format
    
*   Quality-of-life improvements for Hytale workflow
    
*   Texture painting and UV mapping
    
*   Real-time preview
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#official-art-style-guidelines)

Official Art Style Guidelines:

*   **Primitives:** Only cubes and quads (no spheres!)
    
*   **Texture Density:** 64px/unit for characters, 32px/unit for props/blocks
    
*   **Texture Size:** Multiples of 32px (32, 64, 96, 128, etc.)
    
*   **Stretching Limits:** 0.7X to 1.3X on any axis
    
*   **Colors:** Avoid pure white and pure black
    
*   **Triangle Count:** Keep optimized for performance
    

**Official Models:** [Download Examplesarrow-up-right](https://cdn.hytale.com/Hytale%20Model%20Examples.zip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#getting-started)

Getting Started:

1.  Download Blockbench from the official website
    
2.  Install the Hytale Blockbench plugin
    
3.  Study official model examples
    
4.  Follow [Blockbench Modeling Guide](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/17-blockbench-modeling-guide)
    
5.  Export in Hytale format
    
6.  Place files in your Pack's `Common/` folder
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#file-formats)

File Formats:

*   **Models:** `.blockymodel` - Custom block/item models
    
*   **Animations:** `.blockyanim` - Block animation files
    
*   **Textures:** `.png` - Standard PNG images (multiples of 32px)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#hytale-asset-editor)

Hytale Asset Editor

**Access:** Built into Hytale (Creation Tools tab) **Official Info:** [Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

**Description:** Visual editor for data assets (JSON files). Supports most asset types with some limitations.

**Status:** Available now in Early Access

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#features-1)

Features:

*   Edit data assets visually (no coding required)
    
*   Supports blocks, items, and most asset types
    
*   Direct integration with Hytale
    
*   Live preview of changes
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#current-limitations)

Current Limitations:

*   Notable limitations around NPCs
    
*   World generation editing limited
    
*   Interactions not fully exposed
    
*   **Note:** Will expand over time
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#use-cases)

Use Cases:

*   Modify block properties
    
*   Configure item behaviors
    
*   Edit asset metadata
    
*   Visual asset configuration
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#asset-graph-editor-node-editor)

Asset Graph Editor (Node Editor)

**Access:** Built into Hytale (after launch) **Official Info:** [World Generation Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2026/1/the-future-of-world-generation)

**Description:** Node-based editor for complex assets like world generation, NPCs, and creative tool brushes.

**Status:** Currently being released

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#features-2)

Features:

*   Visual node-graph interface
    
*   Live-reload in-game
    
*   No coding required
    
*   Build advanced procedural content by linking simple nodes
    
*   Full control over biomes, terrain, props, and materials
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#use-cases-1)

Use Cases:

*   World generation (biomes, terrain, props)
    
*   NPC behavior configuration
    
*   Creative tool brush creation
    
*   Complex asset configuration
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#world-generation-capabilities)

World Generation Capabilities:

*   **Pattern Scanning System** - Contextual prop placement
    
*   **Terrain Shape Control** - Independent biome terrain
    
*   **Material Providers** - Control terrain materials
    
*   **Props System** - POIs, vegetation, decorations
    
*   **Live-Reload** - Instant in-game feedback
    

**Note:** Internal tool being made public - expect rough edges but useful functionality.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#creative-mode-tools)

Creative Mode Tools

**Access:** Built into Hytale (Creative Mode) **Official Info:** [Creative Mode Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-creative-mode)

**Description:** Interactive suite of in-game tools for world editing and content creation.

**Status:** Available in Early Access

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#tools-available)

Tools Available:

*   **Scripted Brushes** - Asset-defined brushes (mountains, paths, ruins)
    
*   **Shape Brush** - Paint pyramids, cones, squares, and more
    
*   **Selection Tool** - 3D selections, copy, paste, move, rotate
    
*   **Paste Tool** - Precise prefab placement
    
*   **Ruler Tool** - Measure distances and mark outlines
    
*   **Laser Pointer** - Point out locations to friends
    
*   **Machinima Tool** - Camera animation and recording
    
*   **Prefab Browser/Editor** - Browse and edit prefabs
    
*   **Player Model Changer** - Become any NPC model
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#creative-mode-features)

Creative Mode Features:

*   Customizable flight (speed, controls, inertia)
    
*   Quick Settings Panel
    
*   Help Menu for commands
    
*   Real-time world modification
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#machinima-tools)

Machinima Tools

**Access:** Built into Hytale **Official Info:** [Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

**Description:** Tools used to create the official 2018 Hytale trailer. Create cinematic content with camera animations.

**Status:** Available but needs technical fixes

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#features-3)

Features:

*   Camera actor placement
    
*   Keyframe animation
    
*   Speed and timing control
    
*   Cinematic recording
    

**Note:** Scheduled for massive upgrade in functionality and UX after launch.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#community-resources)

Community Resources


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#hytaleguide.net)

HytaleGuide.net ⭐

**Website:** [https://hytaleguide.netarrow-up-right](https://hytaleguide.net/)
 **Forum:** [Community Forumarrow-up-right](https://hytaleguide.net/)

**Description:** Comprehensive wiki dedicated to Hytale gameplay content, items, mobs, zones, and adventure mode information.

**Content:**

*   **Items Database** - Weapons, armor, food, and item stats
    
*   **Mobs Encyclopedia** - Creature information, drops, and locations
    
*   **Zones Guide** - Emerald Grove, Borea, Devastated Lands, Howling Sands
    
*   **Biomes Information** - Biome-specific content and features
    
*   **Alterverses** - Information about Orbis and other planets
    
*   **Guides Section** - Gameplay guides and tutorials
    
*   **Community Forum** - Discussion and server listings
    

**Perfect for:**

*   Learning about Hytale gameplay content
    
*   Understanding items, mobs, and zones
    
*   Adventure mode information
    
*   Community discussions and server listings
    

**Note:** Focuses on gameplay content rather than modding - complementary to modding documentation.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#hytale-modding-documentation)

Hytale Modding Documentation

**Website:** [https://hytalemodding.devarrow-up-right](https://hytalemodding.dev/en/docs)
 **GitHub:** [HytaleModding/sitearrow-up-right](https://github.com/HytaleModding/site)

**Description:** Community-driven documentation site providing comprehensive guides and resources for Hytale modding. Open source and accepting contributions.

**Content:**

*   **Quick Start** - Setting up a standard Hytale project
    
*   **Learning to Learn** - Meta-learning guide for becoming a better learner
    
*   **3D Modeling Guides** - Fundamentals, techniques, and best practices
    
*   **Java Basics Series** - Programming tutorials for beginners
    
*   **Publishing Your Mod** - How to distribute mods
    
*   **Established Information** - Core modding concepts and FAQ
    
*   **Contributing** - How to contribute to their documentation
    

**Philosophy:**

> "It is important to note that modding Hytale is not restricted to programming plugins. Programming, visual scripting, texturing, 3D modelling, modifying assets, etc. are all modding. In Hytale, anyone can be a modder."

**Perfect for:**

*   Beginners learning Java programming
    
*   Those looking for community-driven tutorials
    
*   Modders wanting to publish their work
    
*   Contributors who want to help improve documentation
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#hytale-modding-video-tutorials)

Hytale Modding Video Tutorials

**YouTube Playlist:** [Modding by Kaupenjoearrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLKGarocXCE1EBIOx2UTpGPZyWMpanSnDj)

**Description:** Comprehensive video tutorial series covering Hytale modding from basics to advanced topics.

**Content:**

*   Step-by-step video guides
    
*   Visual demonstrations
    
*   Practical examples
    
*   Beginner-friendly explanations
    
*   Advanced techniques and patterns
    

**Perfect for:** Visual learners who prefer video tutorials over written documentation.

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#development-tools)

Development Tools


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#intellij-idea)

IntelliJ IDEA

**Website:** [https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/arrow-up-right](https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/)

**Description:** The recommended IDE for Java plugin development.

**Versions:**

*   **Community Edition:** Free, sufficient for Hytale plugin development
    
*   **Ultimate Edition:** Paid, includes additional features
    

**Why IntelliJ:**

*   Excellent Java support
    
*   Built-in Gradle integration
    
*   Powerful debugging tools
    
*   Code completion and refactoring
    
*   Integration with version control
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#java-development-kit-jdk)

Java Development Kit (JDK)

**Required Version:** Java 25

**Download:**

*   **Oracle JDK:** [https://www.oracle.com/java/arrow-up-right](https://www.oracle.com/java/)
    
*   **OpenJDK:** [https://openjdk.org/arrow-up-right](https://openjdk.org/)
    

**Note:** Hytale plugins require Java 25 specifically.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#gradle)

Gradle

**Website:** [https://gradle.org/arrow-up-right](https://gradle.org/)

**Description:** Build automation tool used for compiling and packaging Hytale plugins.

**Features:**

*   Dependency management
    
*   Build automation
    
*   Plugin packaging
    
*   Task execution
    

**Note:** Usually included with plugin templates, manual installation not typically required.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#custom-gradle-plugin-for-server-testing)

Custom Gradle Plugin for Server Testing

**Documentation:** [Gradle Automation & Testing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/13-gradle-automation-testing)

**Description:** Custom Gradle plugin that automates the entire development workflow: build, deploy, and test your plugin on a Hytale server with a single command.

**Features:**

*   Automatic server JAR download and caching
    
*   Compiles and deploys your plugin automatically
    
*   Starts server with interactive console
    
*   One-command workflow: `./gradlew runServer`
    
*   Saves hours of manual testing time
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Rapid plugin development and testing
    
*   Automated CI/CD pipelines
    
*   Multi-version server testing
    
*   Remote debugging support
    

**Learn More:** See the complete implementation guide in [Gradle Automation & Testing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/13-gradle-automation-testing)
.

*   Share your mods with the community

*   Issue tracking
    
*   Free for public and private repositories

*   Bytecode injection

Getting Help


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#when-youre-stuck)

When You're Stuck:

1.  **Check Documentation:** Review the official tutorials first
    
2.  **Search Community Forums:** Someone may have asked your question
    
3.  **Ask the Community:** Join Hytale modding communities
    
4.  **Check Examples:** Look at vanilla assets or other mods
    
5.  **Read Error Logs:** They often contain helpful information
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools#how-to-ask-good-questions)

How to Ask Good Questions:

*   Describe what you're trying to achieve
    
*   Show what you've tried
    
*   Include error messages
    
*   Provide relevant code/JSON
    
*   Mention your environment (OS, Java version, etc.)

# Getting Started with Packs | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Getting Started with Packsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:01 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide walks you through creating your first Hytale Pack. Packs are asset/content packs that allow you to add new blocks, items, mobs, and behavior to Hytale without requiring coding knowledge.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#step-1-creating-a-folder)

Step 1: Creating a Folder


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, create a folder for your Pack:

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName`

Replace `YourPackName` with the desired name of your Pack.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#example)

Example:

Copy

    C:\Users\YourUsername\AppData\Roaming\Hytale\UserData\Packs\MyFirstPack

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#step-2-manifest-file)

Step 2: Manifest File


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a `manifest.json` file in your Pack folder. This file contains metadata about your Pack.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#manifest-template)

Manifest Template:

Copy

    {
      "Group": "YourGroupName",
      "Name": "PackName",
      "Version": "1.0.0",
      "Description": "Add the pack description here",
      "Authors": [\
        {\
          "Name": "AuthorName",\
          "Email": "example@example.com",\
          "Url": "https://your-url.com"\
        }\
      ],
      "Website": "https://your-website.com",
      "ServerVersion": "*",
      "Dependencies": {},
      "OptionalDependencies": {},
      "DisabledByDefault": false
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#manifest-fields-explained)

Manifest Fields Explained:

Field

Description

Required

`Group`

Your organization or group name

Yes

`Name`

The name of your Pack

Yes

`Version`

Version number (semantic versioning)

Yes

`Description`

A brief description of what your Pack does

Yes

`Authors`

Array of author information

Yes

`Website`

Your website or project page

Optional

`ServerVersion`

Compatible server version (`*` for all)

Yes

`Dependencies`

Packs required for this to work

Optional

`OptionalDependencies`

Packs that enhance but aren't required

Optional

`DisabledByDefault`

Whether Pack loads automatically

Optional

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#step-3-common-and-server-folders)

Step 3: Common and Server Folders


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create two main folders inside your Pack directory:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#folder-structure)

Folder Structure:

Copy

    ./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/
    |-- manifest.json
    |-- Common/
    `-- Server/

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#common-folder)

Common Folder

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Common`

**Handles:**

*   Models
    
*   Textures
    
*   Visual assets
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#server-folder)

Server Folder

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Server`

**Handles:**

*   Item creation
    
*   Block creation
    
*   Translations
    
*   Particle creation
    
*   Game logic and behavior
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#complete-folder-structure-example)

Complete Folder Structure Example


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    MyFirstPack/
    |-- manifest.json
    |-- Common/
    |   |-- BlockTextures/
    |   |-- Icons/
    |   `-- Models/
    `-- Server/
        |-- Item/
        |   |-- Items/
        |   `-- Category/
        |-- Languages/
        |   `-- en-US/
        `-- Block/

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#next-steps)

Next Steps


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now that you have the basic Pack structure set up, you can:

1.  **Add a Block** - Follow the "Adding a Block" tutorial
    
2.  **Create Item Categories** - Follow the "Item Categories" tutorial
    
3.  **Learn about Block Hitboxes** - Follow the "Block Hitboxes" tutorial
    
4.  **Use the Asset Editor** - Modify your Pack settings in-game
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation#activating-your-pack)

Activating Your Pack


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use your Pack in Hytale:

1.  Open Hytale
    
2.  Go to the "Worlds" tab
    
3.  Right-click on the world you wish to add the Pack to
    
4.  Toggle on your Pack from the list
    
5.  Enter the world to see your changes
    

* * *
